Copilot 2026/04/17 15:45

主判断

上次会话之后，你的研究最该升级的地方，不是再补一条证据，而是把 CT39 从一个 39 基因交集模块，升级成一个可检验的状态转移模型。现在的 [cross_CT39_bridge.ipynb](cross_CT39_bridge.ipynb) 已经把 GRN、trajectory、LIANA 和 spatial 四块摆出来了，但它目前主要回答的是“CT39 在每个维度里有没有信号”。更强的问题应该改成：

CT39 是否标记了 TAM 从 hypoxia sensing 到 immunosuppressive execution 的过渡态，并在空间上与肿瘤内在代谢轴形成互补生态位。

这样一改，[cross_project_meta/CT39_integrated_evidence_chain.md](cross_project_meta/CT39_integrated_evidence_chain.md)、[cross_project_meta/CT39_research_roadmap_reframed.md](cross_project_meta/CT39_research_roadmap_reframed.md) 和 [cross_project_meta/CT39_validation_plan.md](cross_project_meta/CT39_validation_plan.md) 才会真正收束成一条主线，而不是几份都强、但彼此还有一点平行的文档。

我建议你把整体叙事改成双轴模型。第一条轴是髓系重编程轴：HIF1A 先把 TAM 推入应激起点，随后 NFκB 不是简单整体上升，而是分成更偏免疫抑制的支和更偏炎症的支，最后落到 SPP1 和 APOE 这类效应分子，并真正改变 T 细胞通讯。第二条轴是肿瘤内在代谢轴：TPI1、TEAD1、SOX11、FOXN3 这一组更像肿瘤核心的代谢和发育程序，不该再硬塞回 CT39 下面。你前一轮结果其实已经提示这一点了，所以更强的写法不是把 TPI1 说成 HIF1A 下游，而是把它定义成与 CT39 平行、但空间上互补的肿瘤轴。这样整篇文章会从“一个大而全的混合故事”变成“免疫轴 + 肿瘤轴 + 空间接口”的结构，明显更稳。

如果继续加强研究思路，我认为最关键的是把三个竞争模型主动写进主线。第一，CT39 不是单纯的 TAM abundance proxy，否则校正 myeloid infiltration 之后信号就该塌。第二，CT39 不是单纯的 hypoxia core marker，否则它只会跟低氧共定位，不会稳定带出通讯输出和分支顺序。第三，CT39 不是 terminal SPP1 label，否则它不该在时间上先于或早于终末免疫抑制状态出现。只要你把这三个反证逻辑明确写进 bridge notebook 和论文 Results，整条主线就会从“描述性整合”变成“带有排他性的机制模型”。

所以，[cross_CT39_bridge.ipynb](cross_CT39_bridge.ipynb) 最值得升级的，不是再加更多维度，而是把现有四段改成四个桥接预测：上游锚定，证明 CT39 接在 HIF1A 和特定 NFκB 分支后面；过渡态证明，证明它不是终末标签而是分支前后的桥；输出层证明，证明 CT39 high TAM 的通讯后果是免疫抑制增强、共刺激减弱；空间层证明，证明它占据的是 TAM 与肿瘤程序相遇的生态位，而不是纯肿瘤核心或纯坏死边界。最后再单独放一个 competing models 小节，把 abundance、hypoxia-only、SPP1-terminal 这三种替代解释依次打掉。这样这个 notebook 就会从“桥接展示”升级成“桥接论证”。

优先级上，我会这样排。第一，先把 CT39 明确定义为 transition state，而不是 module。第二，把 TPI1 这条线从 CT39 叙事里拆出来，作为并行 tumor intrinsic axis。第三，补患者和分子亚型层面的异质性解释，因为这是你最强结果最容易被追问的地方。第四，再去做更贵的验证，比如 velocity、CellOracle 或更重的表观层分析。换句话说，你现在最缺的不是数据量，而是把已有结果重新压缩成一个更难被反驳的科学问题。

sn_labels = {

**Column Names in adata.obs:**

- tissue_unified or tissue_type: **"Peritumoral"** or **"Tumor"**
- subtype (manual annotation above)
- dominant_program: Top-scoring molecular program from program score matrix

Directory: /scGBM/write/5_myeloid_subclustering_v2

- cluster (leiden_sub)

- Peritumoral, Tumor: cell counts
- tissue_type

#### **Spatial/Multi-omics**
- region: Peri/Tumor classification
- Programs scored via: sc.tl.score_genes()

**39 Human Genes (Cross-species Conserved Hypoxia-Stress TAM genes):**

AFF4, ATF3, CCL4L2, CDK14, CREB5, CREM, DUSP1, EPB41L3, FOSL2, FTH1,

**Availability in datasets:**
- SCENIC regulon targets: **30/39** available

**Key genes in CT39:**
- **HIF1A-associated:** VEGFA, SLC2A1 (glycolysis/hypoxia)

### **4. HIF1A_SCORE & NFKB1_SCORE COMPUTATION METHODS**

**Method:** sc.tl.score_genes() (from Scanpy)

#### **Exact Code Pattern** (from [CT39_permutation_test.ipynb](CT39_permutation_test.ipynb) lines 945-947, [cross_project_summary2.ipynb](cross_project_summary2.ipynb) lines 1858-1866):

# HIF1A score (hypoxia/stress genes)
avail_hif = [g for g in hif1a_genes if g in adata.var_names]
sc.tl.score_genes(adata, gene_list=avail_hif, score_name='HIF1A_score', 
                   use_raw=False, ctrl_size=50)

# NFκB score (inflammatory/NF-κB pathway genes)  
avail_nfk = [g for g in nfkb_genes if g in adata.var_names]
sc.tl.score_genes(adata, gene_list=avail_nfk, score_name='NFkB_score',
                   use_raw=False, ctrl_size=50)

# CT39 module score
sc.tl.score_genes(adata, gene_list=ct39_genes, score_name='CT39_score',
                   use_raw=False, ctrl_size=50)

**Parameters:**
- use_raw=False: Use **log1p-normalized, highly variable genes** (not raw counts)
- ctrl_size=50: Control size for background gene sampling
- **Output:** New columns in adata.obs: HIF1A_score, NFkB_score, CT39_score

**Gene Sets Used:**
- **HIF1A pathway genes:** VEGFA, SLC2A1, LDHA, PGK1, ALDOA, ENO1, PDK1, ... (~15-20 genes)
- **NFκB pathway genes:** REL, RELA, RELB, NFKB1, NFKB2, TNF, IL6, IL1B, ... (~15-20 genes)
- **Regulon AUC:** From pySCENIC, stored as direct matrix columns (e.g., HIF1A(+), NFKB1(+))

---

### **5. TISSUE/RECURRENCE CATEGORIES**

#### **Spatial Classes (Primary GBM):**
- **"Peritumoral"** (Edge): adata.obs['tissue_type'] == 'Peritumoral'
- 9,813 cells in trajectory
- Peri-dominant subtypes: Homeostatic MG, C1Q-MG, Phago/AP-MG
- **"Tumor"** (Core): adata.obs['tissue_type'] == 'Tumor'
- ~15,000 cells in trajectory
- Tumor-dominant subtypes: BMDM-TAM, Inflammatory TAM

#### **Temporal/Recurrence Classes (Recurrent GBM - GSE174554):**
From [cross_project_summary2.ipynb](cross_project_summary2.ipynb#L2400-L2450):

# Temporal progression categories
conditions = ['Primary', '1st Recurrent', '2nd Recurrent']
adata.obs['timepoint'] = ['Primary', '1stRec', '2ndRec']

# Proportion tracking columns in summary tables:
['pct_Primary', 'pct_1stRec', 'pct_2ndRec']

**Observed Progression:**
- **Primary GBM**: Low HIF1A-high × NFκB-high co-expression
- **1st Recurrent**: Moderate increase
- **2nd Recurrent**: **2.93× increase** (→ tipping point; lines 1208-1215)

---

### **6. "TIPPING POINT" DEFINITION**

#### **Double-Positive Cell Threshold (from [CT39_permutation_test.ipynb](CT39_permutation_test.ipynb) lines 1056-1063, 1156-1215):**

# Define "double-positive" cells:
hif_q3  = adata.obs['HIF1A_score'].quantile(0.75)      # 75th percentile
nfk_q3  = adata.obs['NFkB_score'].quantile(0.75)       # 75th percentile

# "Double-High" = top 25% in BOTH HIF1A AND NFκB
double_high = (adata.obs['HIF1A_score'] > hif_q3) & (adata.obs['NFkB_score'] > nfk_q3)

# Tipping point = proportional jump in double-high cells
# Primary → 1stRec → 2ndRec shows accelerating fold-change
# TRUE tipping point occurs at 1st → 2nd Recurrent (2.93× fold change)

**Biological Interpretation:**
- **Cells with simultaneous hypoxia + inflammatory stress**
- **Criteria:** Both HIF1A_score AND NFκB_score > 75th percentile
- **Tipping occurs:** When ~10% of TAM population crosses threshold → positive feedback cascade
- **Evidence:** [CT39_permutation_test.ipynb](CT39_permutation_test.ipynb#L1215) mentions "positive feedback amplification"

'CT39_score'].values\\n\",\n    \"    if len(pri) > 10 and len(rec) > 10:\\n\",\n    \"        u, p = mannwhitneyu(rec, pri, alternative='greater')  # 单侧: 复发 > 原发\\n\",\n    \"        r = u / rec.mean(),\\n\",\n    \"                       'delta': rec.mean() - pri.mean(), 'rank_biserial': r, 'pval': p})\\n\",\n    \"\\n\",\n    \"df_test = pd.DataFrame(results)\\n\",\n \"source\": [\n    \"## §10 CT39 Decomposition: 总体变化 = 比例效应 + 激活效应\"\n   ]\n  },\n  {\n   \"cell_type\": \"code\",\n   \"execution_count\": null,\n   \"metadata\": {},\n   \"outputs\": [],\n   \"source\": [\n    \"# Oaxaca-Blinder 式分解:\\n\",\n    \"# Δ_total = Σ (w2_i × s2_i) - Σ (w1_i × s1_i)\\n\",\n    \"# = Σ (Δw_i × s̄_i)  [比例效应]  +  Σ (w̄_i × Δs_i)  [激活效应]\\n\",\n    \"\\n\",\n    \"subtypes = df_sum['subtype'].values\\n\",\n    \"w1 = df_sum['prop_Primary'].values  # Primary 比例\\n\",\n    \"w2 = df_sum['prop_2ndRecur'].values  # 2nd Recur 比例\\n\",\n    \"s1 = df_sum['CT39_Primary'].values  # Primary CT39\\n\",\n    \"s2 = df_sum['CT39_2ndRecur'].values  # 2nd Recur CT39\\n\",\n    \"\\n\",\n    \"total_change = (w2 * s2).sum() - (w1 * s1).sum()\\n\",\n    \"composition_effect = ((w2 - w1) * (s1 + s2) / 2).sum()  # 比例效应\\n\",\n    \"activation_effect = (((w1 + w2) / 2) * (s2 - s1)).sum()  # 激活效应\\n\",\n    \"\\n\",\n    \"print(f'CT39 总变化 (2nd Recur - Primary): {total_change:.4f}')\\n\",\n    \"print(f'  比例效应 (composition): {composition_effect:.4f} ({composition_effect/total_change:.0%})')\\n\",\n    \"print(f'  激活效应 (activation):  {activation_effect:.4f} ({activation_effect/total_change:.0%})')\\n\",\n    \"\\n\",\n    \"# 逐亚型分解\\n\",\n    \"df_sum['comp_effect'] = (w2 - w1) * (s1 + s2) / 2\\n\",\n    \"df_sum['act_effect'] = ((w1 + w2) / 2) * (s2 - s1)\\n\",\n    \"print('\\\\n逐亚型分解:')\\n\",\n    \"print(df_sum[['subtype', 'comp_effect', 'act_effect']].round(4).to_string(index=False))\"\n   ]\n  },\n  {\n   \"cell_type\": \"code\",\n   \"execution_count\": null,\n   \"metadata\": {},\n   \"outputs\": [],\n   \"source\": [\n    \"# Stacked bar: 比例效应 vs 激活效应\\n\",\n    \"fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(5, 4))\\n\",\n dp_wide[['Primary', '1st Recur', '2nd Recur']]\ndp_wide['fold_2nd_vs_P'] = dp_wide['2nd Recur'] / dp_wide['Primary'].replace(0, np.nan)\nprint('\\nDP fraction by subtype × timepoint:')\nprint(dp_wide.round(4).to_string())\n\n# Decomposition\nsummary = []\nfor mc in adata.obs['Minor_cluster'].unique():\n    sub = adata.obs[adata.obs['Minor_cluster'] == mc]\n    pri = sub[sub['timepoint'] == 'Primary']\n    rec2 = sub[sub['timepoint'] == '2nd Recur']\n    if len(pri) < 10 or len(rec2) < 5:\n        continue\n    n_pri_total = (adata.obs['timepoint'] == 'Primary').sum()\n    n_rec2_total = (adata.obs['timepoint'] == '2nd Recur').sum()\n    summary.append({'subtype': mc, 'prop_Primary': len(pri)/n_pri_total,\n                   'prop_2ndRecur': len(rec2)/n_rec2_total,\n                   'prop_change': len(rec2)/n_rec2_total - len(pri)/n_pri_total,\n                   'CT39_Primary': pri['CT39_score'].mean(),\n                   'CT39_2ndRecur': rec2['CT39_score'].mean(),\n                   'CT39_delta': rec2['CT39_score'].mean() - pri['CT39_score'].mean()})\n\ndf_sum = pd.DataFrame(summary).sort_values('CT39_delta', ascending=False)\nw1, w2 = df_sum['prop_Primary'].values, df_sum['prop_2ndRecur'].values\ns1, s2 = df_sum['CT39_Primary'].values, df_sum['CT39_2ndRecur'].values\ntotal_change = (w2 * s2).sum() - (w1 * s1).sum()\ncomp_eff = ((w2 - w1) * (s1 + s2) / 2).sum()\nact_eff = (((w1 + w2) / 2) * (s2 - s1)).sum()\nprint(f'\\n=== Decomposition ===')\nprint(f'Total Δ = {total_change:.4f}')\nprint(f'  Composition = {comp_eff:.4f} ({comp_eff/total_change:.0%})')\nprint(f'  Activation  = {act_eff:.4f} ({act_eff/total_change:.0%})')\nprint('\\nPer-subtype:')\nprint(df_sum[['subtype','prop_change','CT39_delta']].round(4).to_string(index=False))\n\n# Save all CSVs\nct39_by_sub.to_csv(f'{WRITE_DIR}/CT39_by_TAM_subtype.csv')\nct39_sub_tp.to_csv(f'{WRITE_DIR}/CT39_subtype_x_timepoint.csv')\ndf_test.to_csv(f'{WRITE_DIR}/CT39_MWU_primary_vs_recurrent.csv', index=False)\ndp_wide.to_csv(f'{WRITE_DIR}/double_positive_subtype_x_timepoint.csv')\ndf_sum.to_csv(f'{WRITE_DIR}/proportion_vs_activation_decomposition.csv', index=False)\nadata.obs.to_csv(f'{WRITE_DIR}/adata_obs_with_scores.csv.gz', compression='gzip')\n\nprint(f'\\nAll CSVs saved to {WRITE_DIR}')\nprint('=== DONE ===')\nPYEOF\n",

全部分析完成。核心发现总结：

## Subtype × CT39 分析结果

**核心发现：**

| 发现 | 数据 |
|------|------|
| **CT39 最高亚型** | Hypoxia TAM (0.59) >> Inflammatory TAM (0.42) >> 其余 (~0.13-0.17) |
| **复发飙升最猛** | Hypoxia TAM: 0.505 → 0.986 (Δ=0.48, 2nd Recur) |
| **全亚型收敛** | Primary 时 6 亚型差距 6× (0.08-0.51)；2nd Recur 收窄至 2.5× (0.40-0.99) |
| **DP 爆发** | Scavenger-IS/Homeostatic MG 在 2nd Recur DP fraction 飙升 **12-13 倍** |
| **分解** | 总 CT39 上升由 Composition (Hypoxia/Inflammatory 比例↑) + Activation (全亚型激活↑) 双驱动 |
| **snGBM 验证** | BMDM-TAM CT39 最高 (0.35)；所有 9 个 cluster Tumor > Peritumoral 显著 |

**输出：** 6 个 CSV + 9 张图 → [write/cross_subtype_CT39/](write/cross_subtype_CT39/)

Copilot 2026/04/17 16:28

---

## 项目全景梳理

### 你手里有什么

**4 个 GBM 单细胞数据集**，各自承担一个维度：

| 数据集 | 角色 | 髓系细胞数 |
|--------|------|-----------|
| scGBM (scRNA) | 基线图谱 + SCENIC regulon 发现 | 75K |
| 复发GBM (scRNA) | **时间维度**: Primary → 1st Rec → 2nd Rec | 120K |
| Mouse GBM (scRNA) | **空间维度**: Tumor core vs Periphery | 27K |
| snGBM (snRNA + snATAC) | 技术验证 + 表观遗传 | 18K + 64K |

### 核心发现是什么

**一句话**: CT39 模块（39 基因, HIF1A∩NFκB 交集）是唯一同时在空间和时间两个维度都富集的分子程序。

**双阶段重编程模型**:
1. **Stage 1 空间启动** — HIF1A 即刻靶基因激活 → 糖酵解 +0.486，NFκB 尚未耦合
2. **Stage 2 时间强化** — HIF1A×NFκB coupling 从 ρ≈0 → +0.213，双阳性细胞从 5.8% 跃升至 22.8% (tipping point)

### 已完成分析的层级关系

层级1: 各数据集独立分析 (亚聚类、注释、SCENIC)
  ↓
层级2: 跨项目核心验证 (cross_project_summary §1-§9)
  ├── 亚型映射、CT39 发现、5 模块景观
  ├── Hypoxia TAM 深度表型
  ├── NFκB 时间特异性、4 数据集整合
  └── 证据叙事
  ↓
层级3: 统计鲁棒性 (CT39_permutation_test)
  ├── Permutation Z=6.5 / Z=3.7
  ├── IFN 偏差修复
  ├── Double-positive tipping point
  └── 患者异质性 (62% 一致)
  ↓
层级4: 散落的补充分析 (cross_*.ipynb × 10+)
  ├── SCENIC×轨迹×免疫
  ├── 因果方向推断
  ├── CellRank / Deconvolution
  ├── Subtype × CT39 交互 ← 刚做完
  └── 空间转录组 / snATAC / 多模态整合

### 当前的乱在哪

1. **层级4太散** — 10+ 个 cross_ notebook 各自回答了零散问题，但没有统一到一条故事线上
2. **多个叙事文档并存** — cross_project_research_report.md、direction_C_complete_narrative.md、revised_core_narrative.md、CT39_integrated_evidence_chain.md、direction_ABC_layman_summary.md 等 7 个 .md 文档，内容有大量重叠
3. **核心报告 (§1-§9) 相对完整**，但层级4的分析结果没有被统一整合回来
4. **缺少一个清晰的"论文 Figure 清单"** — 不知道哪些图是主图、哪些是补充

|---|---|---|
| **标题** | 胶质瘤单细胞RNA测序数据整合分析 — 三数据集 | 三数据集 Harmony 整合分析 |
| **数据集 1** | GSE162631 (4 patients, Tumor/Peritumoral) | GSE162631 (同) |
| **数据集 2** | GSE273274 (3 patients, GBM centre/surround) | GSE273274 (同) |
| **数据集 3** | **GSE241037** — 4 GBM patients, 10X CD45+ FACS, Core/Periphery; ⚠️ 跳过小鼠样本 | **GSE274987** — 10 patients (~24 samples), **Multiome + ParseBio**, PT+TC; 排除 TE (Tumor Edge ~50k cells) |
| **MT 上限** | 10% | 20% |
| **Leiden** | [0.5, 0.8, 1.0] | [0.1, 0.5, 0.8, 1.0] |
| **输出目录** | write/0_integrate_scRNAdata | write/0_integrate_three_datasets |

**一句话总结**：两个 notebook 共享前两个数据集 (GSE162631 + GSE273274)，但第三个数据集不同 — _two 用的是 GSE241037 (CD45+ FACS 分选), _three_datasets 用的是 GSE274987 (Multiome + ParseBio 多模态)。两者都没有被执行过。

Copilot 2026/04/17 16:47

**GSE241037 vs GSE274987 的核心区别**:

| 维度 | GSE241037 (CD45+ FACS) | GSE274987 (Multiome + ParseBio) |
|------|----------------------|-------------------------------|
| **细胞富集** | **CD45+ FACS 分选** → 只保留免疫细胞，没有肿瘤细胞和基质细胞 | **无预选** → 包含所有细胞类型（肿瘤、免疫、基质） |
| **样本量** | 4 位 GBM 患者 | 10 位患者, ~24 样本 |
| **技术平台** | 标准 10X Chromium scRNA-seq | Multiome (同一个核同时测 RNA + ATAC) + ParseBio (组合索引, 非微流控) |
| **区域定义** | Core / Periphery | PT (Peritumoral) / TC (Tumor Core), 排除 TE (Tumor Edge) |
| **多组学** | 仅转录组 | RNA + ATAC 配对数据 |

**对你分析的影响**:

1. **如果目标是 TAM 重编程研究** — GSE241037 的 CD45+ 分选意味着你拿到的**纯免疫细胞**，不需要再从全局数据里挑免疫亚群，但**完全缺失肿瘤细胞和 CAF 信息**（做不了 cell-cell communication 的完整分析）
2. **如果要做瘤旁 vs 肿瘤全景分析** — GSE274987 更合适，因为保留了所有细胞类型，且有 scATAC 提供表观遗传信息
3. **批次效应复杂度** — GSE274987 混合了两种完全不同的平台 (Multiome vs ParseBio)，整合难度更高

简单来说：**GSE241037 = 免疫细胞专精视角**，**GSE274987 = 全细胞类型 + 多组学视角**。

Copilot 2026/04/17 18:13

是的，marker 基本沿用了之前 2 marker gene.ipynb 里的 GBM 标准三层体系：

| 类别 | 本次 | 之前 | 差异 |
|------|------|------|------|
| Neuron | SYT1, RBFOX1, SNAP25, STMN2 | 同 | - |
| Oligo | MBP, PLP1, MOG, MAG | 同 | - |
| OPC-like | PDGFRA, OLIG1, OLIG2 | 同 | - |
| NPC-like | DCX, CD24, SOX4, SOX11 | 同 | - |
| AC-like | GFAP, AQP4, HOPX, MLC1 | 同 | - |
| MES-like | CHI3L1, VIM, CD44, VEGFA | 同 | - |
| Microglia | P2RY12, CX3CR1, TMEM119 | +CSF1R | 少了 CSF1R |
| TAM/Macro | CD68, SPP1, APOE, TREM2 | 同 | - |
| Mono | S100A8, S100A9, FCN1, VCAN | 同 | - |
| T cell | CD3D, CD3E, CD8A, IL7R | 同 | - |
| Endo | CLDN5, PECAM1, VWF, FLT1 | 同 | - |
| Pericyte | PDGFRB, RGS5, NOTCH3 | +ACTA2 | 少了 ACTA2 |
| **Prolif** | **MKI67, TOP2A, PCNA** | 无 | **新增** |

核心 marker 完全一致（Neftel 2019 肿瘤状态 + 标准 TME marker），仅增加了 Prolif 类别并微调了个别基因数。

打分结果很清晰。接下来根据最高分自动分配粗类，并标记边界 cluster：

▸ Tool calls (1)
edit_notebook_file 
{

  "editType": "insert",

  "language": "python",
  "newCode": "# 按最高分自动分配粗类\ncoarse_assign = df_scores.idxmax(axis=1).to_dict()\nprint(\"自动分配:\")\nfor cl, ct in sorted(coarse_assign.items(), key=lambda x: int(x[0])):\n    scores = df_scores.loc[cl]\n    top_score = scores.max()\n    second_score = scores.nlargest(2).iloc[1]\n    flag = \" ⚠️ 边界\" if (top_score - second_score) < 0.15 else \"\"\n    print(f\"  Cluster {cl:>2s} → {ct:<10s} (top={top_score:.3f}, gap={top_score-second_score:.3f}){flag}\")\n\n# 应用粗分类\nadata.obs['coarse_type'] = adata.obs['leiden'].map(coarse_assign).astype('category')\nadata.obs['coarse_type'].value_counts()"
}

set(valid)\n    status = f\"({len(valid)}/{len(genes)})\"\n    if missing:\n        status += f\" missing: {missing}\"\n    print(f\"  {ct}: {status}\")\n\n# 每个 cluster 的平均得分\nscore_cols = [f'score_{ct}' for ct in gbm_markers_v3]\ndf_v3 = adata.obs.groupby('leiden', observed=False)[score_cols].mean()\ndf_v3.columns = list(gbm_markers_v3.keys())\n\n# 显示 + 自动分配\nassign_v3 = df_v3.idxmax(axis=1).to_dict()\nprint(\"\\n按最高分自动分配:\")\nfor cl in sorted(assign_v3, key=int):\n    scores = df_v3.loc[cl]\n    top = scores.max()\n    second = scores.nlargest(2).iloc[1]\n    flag = \" ⚠️\" if (top - second) < 0.1 else \"\"\n    print(f\"  Cluster {cl:>2s} → {assign_v3[cl]:<16s} (top={top:.3f}, 2nd={scores.nlargest(2).index[1]}={second:.3f}){flag}\")\n\nprint(f\"\\n得分矩阵:\")\nprint(df_v3.round(3).to_string())"
}

Copilot 2026/04/17 19:04

从 UMAP 可以看到核心问题：**CDC 被过度分配**（62,136 cells, 47.6%）。原因是 HLA-DPB1 是 MHC-II 基因，在所有抗原呈递髓系细胞中高表达，不是 cDC 特异的。

实际上 clusters 1, 2 是 TAM/Macrophage，cluster 10 是 Microglia，clusters 4, 5 也是髓系细胞而非 cDC。

Copilot 2026/04/17 19:47

结果很有意义。Cluster 2 的 **Macrophage score 是所有类型中最低的 (-0.214)**，但 **Microglia score 排第二 (0.533)**。

关键 marker 表达显示 cluster 2 实际是 **Microglia/TAM** 特征：
- TREM2 = 1.464（高）、CX3CR1 = 1.039（高）、TMEM119 = 0.465（中）、CD68 = 1.328（高）
- 而 Macrophage 专用标记 FN1 = 0.242、VCAN = 0.289 较低

实际上 cluster 1 和 2 都更偏 **Microglia/TAM** 而非经典 Macrophage。用户提供的 Macrophage marker set（仅 LYZ/FN1/VCAN 3 个基因）太小且不够特异。

GBM 中髓系细胞更适合分为：
- **Microglia**（TMEM119+, CX3CR1+, TREM2+）→ clusters 1, 2, 5, 10, 11
- **Monocyte**（FCN1+, S100A8+）→ clusters 4, 6

Copilot 2026/04/17 20:34

不会坏。UMAP 上 cluster 1 和 2 确实是**不同的空间位置**，说明它们在基因表达上有差异。但这种差异是**亚型级别**的（比如不同活化状态的 TAM），粗分类时归为同一大类是正确的。

有两种处理方式：

**方案 A**：粗分类保持现状（1=Macrophage, 2=Macrophage），后续做 **Myeloid subclustering** 时再细分 TAM 亚型（这是标准流程第 5 步）

**方案 B**：现在就给 1 和 2 不同标签。从表达差异看：
- Cluster 1: CX3CR1↑ TMEM119↑ → 更偏 **Microglia-like TAM**
- Cluster 2: LYZ↑ FN1↑ VCAN↑ → 更偏 **BMDM-like TAM** (骨髓来源)

▸ Tool calls (1)
edit_notebook_file 
{
  "cellId": "#VSC-b607109d",
  "editType": "insertBefore",
  "filePath": "/Users/yuzuan/Downloads/生信技能树月更复现/scGBM/2_marker_gene.ipynb",
  "newCode": "from sklearn.neighbors import KernelDensity\n\ndef enhance_umap(adata, color='cell_type', figsize=(8, 8), size=8,\n                 kde_bandwidth=0.5, contour_level_frac=0.1,\n                 label_fontsize=9, arrow_frac=0.10, palette=None):\n    \"\"\"参考: 生信大杂烩 Scanpy UMAP美化\"\"\"\n    fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=figsize)\n\n    sc.pl.umap(adata, color=color, legend_loc=None, frameon=False,\n               size=size, ax=ax, add_outline=True, palette=palette,\n               outline_width=(0.1, 0.05), show=False)\n\n    umap_coords = adata.obsm['X_umap']\n    categories = adata.obs[color].cat.categories\n    colors = adata.uns.get(f'{color}_colors', [f'C{i}' for i in range(len(categories))])\n\n    for i, ct in enumerate(categories):\n        mask = adata.obs[color] == ct\n        coords = umap_coords[mask]\n        if len(coords) < 30:\n            continue\n\n        # KDE 轮廓线\n        kde = KernelDensity(bandwidth=kde_bandwidth)\n        kde.fit(coords)\n        x_min_ct, x_max_ct = coords[:, 0].min() - 1, coords[:, 0].max() + 1\n        y_min_ct, y_max_ct = coords[:, 1].min() - 1, coords[:, 1].max() + 1\n        xx, yy = np.meshgrid(\n            np.linspace(x_min_ct, x_max_ct, 100),\n            np.linspace(y_min_ct, y_max_ct, 100)\n        )\n        Z = np.exp(kde.score_samples(np.c_[xx.ravel(), yy.ravel()])).reshape(xx.shape)\n        peak = Z.max()\n        if peak > 0:\n            ax.contour(xx, yy, Z, levels=[peak * contour_level_frac],\n                       colors=[colors[i]], linewidths=0.8, alpha=0.6)\n\n        # 智能标签\n        mx, my = np.median(coords, axis=0)\n        ax.text(mx, my, ct, fontsize=label_fontsize, ha='center', va='center',\n                fontweight='bold',\n                bbox=dict(facecolor='white', alpha=0.85, edgecolor='gray',\n                          boxstyle='round,pad=0.3', linewidth=0.5))\n\n    # 科研风箭头坐标轴\n    x_all, y_all = umap_coords[:, 0], umap_coords[:, 1]\n    x_lo, x_hi = x_all.min(), x_all.max()\n    y_lo, y_hi = y_all.min(), y_all.max()\n    x_range = x_hi - x_lo\n    y_range = y_hi - y_lo\n\n    # 箭头起点 (左下角外侧)\n    ox = x_lo - x_range * 0.02\n    oy = y_lo - y_range * 0.02\n    dx = x_range * arrow_frac\n    dy = y_range * arrow_frac\n    hw = dy * 0.08\n    hl = dx * 0.08\n\n    ax.annotate('', xy=(ox + dx, oy), xytext=(ox, oy),\n                arrowprops=dict(arrowstyle='->', lw=1.5, color='black'))\n    ax.annotate('', xy=(ox, oy + dy), xytext=(ox, oy),\n                arrowprops=dict(arrowstyle='->', lw=1.5, color='black'))\n    ax.text(ox + dx / 2, oy - y_range * 0.03, 'UMAP1',\n            fontsize=10, ha='center', va='top')\n    ax.text(ox - x_range * 0.03, oy + dy / 2, 'UMAP2',\n            fontsize=10, ha='right', va='center', rotation=90)\n\n    ax.set_xlabel('')\n    ax.set_ylabel('')\n    ax.set_title('')\n    plt.tight_layout()\n    return fig, ax\n\nprint('✅ enhance_umap 函数已定义')",

Copilot 2026/04/18 16:20

标签重叠问题。我来给 enhance_umap 加一个标签排斥算法，让重叠的标签自动分开。

▸ Tool calls (1)
edit_notebook_file 
{
  "cellId": "#VSC-eb109cde",
  "editType": "edit",
  "filePath": "/Users/yuzuan/Downloads/生信技能树月更复现/scGBM/2_marker_gene.ipynb",
  "newCode": "from sklearn.neighbors import KernelDensity\n\ndef _repel_labels(positions, min_dist=1.5, iterations=50):\n    \"\"\"简单标签排斥: 让过近的标签互相推开\"\"\"\n    pos = np.array(positions, dtype=float)\n    for _ in range(iterations):\n        moved = False\n        for i in range(len(pos)):\n            for j in range(i + 1, len(pos)):\n                d = pos[j] - pos[i]\n                dist = np.linalg.norm(d)\n                if dist < min_dist and dist > 0:\n                    shift = (min_dist - dist) / 2 * d / dist\n                    pos[i] -= shift\n                    pos[j] += shift\n                    moved = True\n        if not moved:\n            break\n    return pos\n\ndef enhance_umap(adata, color='cell_type', figsize=(8, 8), size=8,\n                 kde_bandwidth=0.5, contour_level_frac=0.1,\n                 label_fontsize=9, arrow_frac=0.10, palette=None,\n                 label_min_dist=2.0):\n    \"\"\"参考: 生信大杂烩 Scanpy UMAP美化 + 标签排斥\"\"\"\n    fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=figsize)\n\n    sc.pl.umap(adata, color=color, legend_loc=None, frameon=False,\n               size=size, ax=ax, add_outline=True, palette=palette,\n               outline_width=(0.1, 0.05), show=False)\n\n    umap_coords = adata.obsm['X_umap']\n    categories = adata.obs[color].cat.categories\n    colors = adata.uns.get(f'{color}_colors', [f'C{i}' for i in range(len(categories))])\n\n    # 先收集所有标签的原始位置\n    label_info = []  # (ct_name, median_x, median_y, color_idx)\n    for i, ct in enumerate(categories):\n        mask = adata.obs[color] == ct\n        coords = umap_coords[mask]\n        if len(coords) < 30:\n            continue\n        mx, my = np.median(coords, axis=0)\n        label_info.append((ct, mx, my, i, coords))\n\n    # 标签排斥\n    raw_positions = [(info[1], info[2]) for info in label_info]\n    adjusted = _repel_labels(raw_positions, min_dist=label_min_dist)\n\n    # 画 KDE 轮廓 + 标签\n    for idx, (ct, _, _, ci, coords) in enumerate(label_info):\n        # KDE 轮廓线\n        kde = KernelDensity(bandwidth=kde_bandwidth)\n        kde.fit(coords)\n        x_min_ct, x_max_ct = coords[:, 0].min() - 1, coords[:, 0].max() + 1\n        y_min_ct, y_max_ct = coords[:, 1].min() - 1, coords[:, 1].max() + 1\n        xx, yy = np.meshgrid(\n            np.linspace(x_min_ct, x_max_ct, 100),\n            np.linspace(y_min_ct, y_max_ct, 100)\n        )\n        Z = np.exp(kde.score_samples(np.c_[xx.ravel(), yy.ravel()])).reshape(xx.shape)\n        peak = Z.max()\n        if peak > 0:\n            ax.contour(xx, yy, Z, levels=[peak * contour_level_frac],\n                       colors=[colors[ci]], linewidths=0.8, alpha=0.6)\n\n        # 标签 (使用排斥后的位置)\n        lx, ly = adjusted[idx]\n        ax.text(lx, ly, ct, fontsize=label_fontsize, ha='center', va='center',\n                fontweight='bold',\n                bbox=dict(facecolor='white', alpha=0.85, edgecolor='gray',\n                          boxstyle='round,pad=0.3', linewidth=0.5))\n\n    # 科研风箭头坐标轴\n    x_all, y_all = umap_coords[:, 0], umap_coords[:, 1]\n    x_lo, x_hi = x_all.min(), x_all.max()\n    y_lo, y_hi = y_all.min(), y_all.max()\n    x_range = x_hi - x_lo\n    y_range = y_hi - y_lo\n\n    ox = x_lo - x_range * 0.02\n    oy = y_lo - y_range * 0.02\n    dx = x_range * arrow_frac\n    dy = y_range * arrow_frac\n\n    ax.annotate('', xy=(ox + dx, oy), xytext=(ox, oy),\n                arrowprops=dict(arrowstyle='->', lw=1.5, color='black'))\n    ax.annotate('', xy=(ox, oy + dy), xytext=(ox, oy),\n                arrowprops=dict(arrowstyle='->', lw=1.5, color='black'))\n    ax.text(ox + dx / 2, oy - y_range * 0.03, 'UMAP1',\n            fontsize=10, ha='center', va='top')\n    ax.text(ox - x_range * 0.03, oy + dy / 2, 'UMAP2',\n            fontsize=10, ha='right', va='center', rotation=90)\n\n    ax.set_xlabel('')\n    ax.set_ylabel('')\n    ax.set_title('')\n    plt.tight_layout()\n    return fig, ax\n\nprint('enhance_umap 函数已定义 (含标签排斥)')"
}

Copilot 2026/04/18 16:23

这篇文章的风格有几个不同：
- **灰色虚线轮廓** (colors='gray', linestyles='--')
- **标签带细胞比例** ({cell_type} ({percentage:.1f}%))
- **标题显示总细胞数** (Overall (n = {n_obs}))
- bandwidth=0.3，无箭头坐标轴

我来融合两篇文章的优点更新函数：

pos[i]\n                dist = np.linalg.norm(d)\n                if dist < min_dist and dist > 0:\n                    shift = (min_dist - dist) / 2 * d / dist\n                    pos[i] -= shift\n                    pos[j] += shift\n                    moved = True\n        if not moved:\n            break\n    return pos\n\ndef enhance_umap(adata, color='cell_type', figsize=(8, 8), size=15,\n                 kde_bandwidth=0.3, contour_level_frac=0.1,\n                 label_fontsize=10, arrow_frac=0.10, palette=None,\n                 label_min_dist=2.0, show_pct=True, show_arrows=True,\n                 contour_color='gray', contour_style='--',\n                 title=None):\n    \"\"\"融合: 生信大杂烩 + 生信星球 UMAP 美化\"\"\"\n    fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=figsize)\n\n    sc.pl.umap(adata, color=color, legend_loc=None, frameon=False,\n               size=size, ax=ax, add_outline=True, palette=palette,\n               outline_width=(0.1, 0.05), show=False)\n\n    umap_coords = adata.obsm['X_umap']\n    categories = adata.obs[color].cat.categories\n    colors_list = adata.uns.get(f'{color}_colors', [f'C{i}' for i in range(len(categories))])\n\n    # 细胞比例\n    ct_counts = adata.obs[color].value_counts(normalize=True) * 100\n\n    # 收集标签位置\n    label_info = []\n    for i, ct in enumerate(categories):\n        mask = adata.obs[color] == ct\n        coords = umap_coords[mask]\n        if len(coords) < 30:\n            continue\n        mx, my = np.median(coords, axis=0)\n        label_info.append((ct, mx, my, i, coords))\n\n    # 标签排斥\n    raw_positions = [(info[1], info[2]) for info in label_info]\n    adjusted = _repel_labels(raw_positions, min_dist=label_min_dist)\n\n    # KDE 轮廓 + 标签\n    for idx, (ct, _, _, ci, coords) in enumerate(label_info):\n        kde = KernelDensity(bandwidth=kde_bandwidth, metric='euclidean')\n        kde.fit(coords)\n        x_min_ct, x_max_ct = coords[:, 0].min() - x_lo\n        y_range = y_hi - y_lo\n        ox = x_lo - x_range * 0.02\n        oy = y_lo - y_range * 0.02\n        dx = x_range * arrow_frac\n        dy = y_range * arrow_frac\n        ax.annotate('', xy=(ox + dx, oy), xytext=(ox, oy),\n                    arrowprops=dict(arrowstyle='->', lw=1.5, color='black'))\n        ax.annotate('', xy=(ox, oy + dy), xytext=(ox, oy),\n                    arrowprops=dict(arrowstyle='->', lw=1.5, color='black'))\n        ax.text(ox + dx / 2, oy - ▸ Tool calls (1)
file_search 
{
  "query": "scGBM/*preprocess*.ipynb"
}
Copilot 2026/04/18 16:51

是的，问题在选中的这段代码里，有两个 bug：

**Bug 1: threshold=0.25 硬编码阈值**

Scrublet 的 doublet_score 在你的数据里最大只到 0.248，而你硬编码了 threshold=0.25，所以**所有细胞都低于阈值，没有任何一个被标为 doublet**。sc.pp.scrublet 默认 threshold=None 时会自动检测双峰分布来确定阈值，你写了 0.25 反而把自动检测给覆盖了。

**Bug 2: expected_doublet_rate 计算公式可以更稳健**

min(n_before * 0.008 / 1000, 0.15) — 数学上正确（10X ~0.8%/1000 cells），但对于小样本（如 <3000 cells）结果会极低（<2.4%），导致模拟的 doublet 不够，Scrublet 检测灵敏度下降。

**修复方案**: 去掉硬编码 threshold，让 Scrublet 自动检测；自动检测失败时 fallback 到保守阈值。

▸ Tool calls (1)

      "title": "诊断 Scrublet 代码问题"
    },
    {
      "id": 2,
      "status": "in-progress",
      "title": "修复 doublet 检测代码"
    },
    {
      "id": 3,
      "status": "not-started",
      "title": "验证修改正确性"
    }
  ]
}
Copilot 2026/04/18 16:53

修改已生效。总结改了什么：

| 原代码 | 修复 |
|--------|------|
| threshold=0.25 硬编码 | 去掉 threshold，让 Scrublet 自动检测双峰 |
| expected_rate 无下限 | 加了 max(..., 0.02) 保底 2% |
| 自动检测失败无兜底 | 加了 fallback: 若自动阈值检出 0 个 doublet，退回 score > 0.2 |

这个 notebook 需要从 Scrublet 那个 cell 开始**重新跑一遍**后续所有 cell（合并 → 归一化 → HVG → PCA → Harmony → UMAP → 保存），然后 2_marker_gene.ipynb 也要重新加载 adata1.h5ad 重跑。

▸ Tool calls (1)
edit_notebook_file 
{
  "cellId": "#VSC-4123836c",
  "editType": "insert",
  "filePath": "/Users/yuzuan/Downloads/生信技能树月更复现/scGBM/3_CNV_validation.ipynb",
  "language": "python",
  "newCode": "# Neuronal clusters vs Tumor vs Immune 的 CNV 分布对比\nfrom scipy.stats import mannwhitneyu\n\nsuspect_cls = ['15', '18']\nknown_tumor_cls = ['8', '9', '17']\nknown_immune_cls = ['0', '3', '6']\n\ntumor_scores = adata.obs.loc[adata.obs['leiden'].isin(known_tumor_cls), 'cnv_score']\nimmune_scores = adata.obs.loc[adata.obs['leiden'].isin(known_immune_cls), 'cnv_score']\n\n# 统计检验\nfor cl in suspect_cls:\n    cl_scores = adata.obs.loc[adata.obs['leiden'] == cl, 'cnv_score']\n    _, p_vs_tumor = mannwhitneyu(cl_scores, tumor_scores, alternative='two-sided')\n    _, p_vs_immune = mannwhitneyu(cl_scores, immune_scores, alternative='two-sided')\n    print(f\"Cluster {cl}: median={cl_scores.median():.4f}, \"\n          f\"vs Tumor p={p_vs_tumor:.2e}, vs Immune p={p_vs_immune:.2e}\")\n\n# Violin plot\ngroups = {\n    'Known_Tumor': known_tumor_cls,\n    'Neuronal_cl15': ['15'],\n    'Neuronal_cl18': ['18'],\n    'Known_Immune': known_immune_cls,\n}\nrecords = []\nfor label, cls in groups.items():\n    mask = adata.obs['leiden'].isin(cls)\n    for s in adata.obs.loc[mask, 'cnv_score']:\n        records.append({'group': label, 'cnv_score': s})\ndf_neuro = pd.DataFrame(records)\n\nfig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(8, 5))\nsns.violinplot(data=df_neuro, x='group', y='cnv_score', ax=ax, inner='box', cut=0)\nax.axhline(y=0.0099, color='red', linestyle='--', alpha=0.6, label='threshold')\nax.set_title('CNV Score: Neuronal clusters 15/18 vs Tumor/Immune')\nax.legend()\nplt.tight_layout()\nplt.savefig(FIG_DIR / 'violin_neuronal_suspect.png', dpi=150, bbox_inches='tight')\nplt.show()"
}

▸ Tool calls (1)
edit_notebook_file 
{
  "cellId": "#VSC-98c7e763",
  "editType": "insert",
  "filePath": "/Users/yuzuan/Downloads/生信技能树月更复现/scGBM/3_CNV_validation.ipynb",
  "language": "python",
  "newCode": "# 可疑 cluster 的 chr7/chr10 区域均值 vs 参考\n# 提取 CNV 矩阵中 chr7 和 chr10 对应的 window\nchr_col = adata.uns['cnv']['chr']  # 每个 window 对应的染色体\nchr7_idx = np.where(chr_col == 'chr7')[0]\nchr10_idx = np.where(chr_col == 'chr10')[0]\nprint(f\"chr7 windows: {len(chr7_idx)}, chr10 windows: {len(chr10_idx)}\")\n\n# 每个 cluster 的 chr7 mean gain 和 chr10 mean loss\nresults = []\nfor cl in sorted(adata.obs['leiden'].unique(), key=int):\n    mask = (adata.obs['leiden'] == cl).values\n    X_cnv = adata.obsm['X_cnv'][mask]\n    chr7_mean = X_cnv[:, chr7_idx].mean()\n    chr10_mean = X_cnv[:, chr10_idx].mean()\n    ct = adata.obs.loc[adata.obs['leiden'] == cl, 'cell_type'].mode()[0]\n    results.append({\n        'cluster': cl, 'cell_type': ct, 'n': mask.sum(),\n        'chr7_gain': chr7_mean, 'chr10_loss': chr10_mean\n    })\n\ndf_chr = pd.DataFrame(results).sort_values('chr7_gain', ascending=False)\nprint(df_chr.to_string(index=False))"
}

  "newCode": "# Cluster 0 (Microglia) 的 CNV score 分布 — 是否双峰？\nfig, axes = plt.subplots(1, 3, figsize=(15, 4))\n\nfor ax, cl, title in zip(axes, ['0', '15', '16'],\n                          ['cl0 Microglia (n=12350)', 'cl15 Neuronal (n=1918)', 'cl16 Oligo (n=2844)']):\n    scores = adata.obs.loc[adata.obs['leiden'] == cl, 'cnv_score']\n    ax.hist(scores, bins=80, color='steelblue', edgecolor='white', linewidth=0.3)\n    ax.axvline(x=0.0099, color='red', linestyle='--', alpha=0.6, label='threshold')\n    ax.set_title(title)\n    ax.set_xlabel('cnv_score')\n    above = (scores > 0.0099).sum()\n    ax.text(0.95, 0.95, f'{above}/{len(scores)} above thr\\n({above/len(scores)*100:.1f}%)',\n            transform=ax.transAxes, ha='right', va='top', fontsize=9,\n            bbox=dict(boxstyle='round', facecolor='wheat', alpha=0.8))\n\nplt.tight_layout()\nplt.savefig(FIG_DIR / 'hist_suspect_cnv_dist.png', dpi=150, bbox_inches='tight')\nplt.show()"
}
Copilot 2026/04/18 19:24

**极其重要的发现！**

| Cluster | 注释 | 超阈值比例 | 判断 |
|---------|------|-----------|------|
| cl15 Neuronal | 96.1% above | **→ 几乎全是肿瘤（NPC-like）** |
| cl16 Oligo | 99.3% above | **→ 几乎全是肿瘤（OPC-like）** |
| cl0 Microglia | **34.3% above** | **→ 双峰分布，混入肿瘤细胞** |

加最终结论和修正建议：

}
Copilot 2026/04/18 19:26

CNV 验证分析完成，UMAP 对比图清晰展示了修正效果。

**核心发现汇总：**

| 修正 | 细胞数 | 依据 |
|------|--------|------|
| Neuronal → **NPC-like Tumor** | 2,232 | 96%+ 超 CNV 阈值 + chr7 gain |
| Oligodendrocyte → **OPC-like Tumor** | 2,844 | 99.3% 超阈值 + chr7 gain |
| Microglia (cl0 部分) → **Tumor** | 4,232 | 双峰分布，34.3% 超阈值 |
| **总计修正** | **9,308 (6.9%)** | |

Copilot 2026/04/19 09:00

确实混乱。核心问题是 **cluster-based 注释产生了 14 个类别**，其中大量过渡态（AC/NPC1、OPC/NPC1、NPC1/NPC2、OPC/AC、Unresolved）在 UMAP 上颜色难以区分且标签重叠。

标准 Neftel 做法是 **per-cell scoring**：对每个细胞打 6 个模块分数，取最高分作为状态标签。这样：
- 干净的 6+1 类（MES1, MES2, AC, OPC, NPC1, NPC2 + Cycling）
- 没有模糊过渡态
- UMAP 清爽很多

我来直接改——在 tumor 注释 cell 后面加一个 scoring-based 注释 cell，替代当前的 cluster-based 结果。

先确认当前 notebook 状态：

▸ Tool calls (1)
copilot_getNotebookSummary 
{
  "filePath": "/Users/yuzuan/Downloads/生信技能树月更复现/scGBM/4_Sub_clustering.ipynb"
}
Copilot 2026/04/19 09:01

现在在 tumor 注释 cell（cell 23）后面插入新的 scoring-based 注释，替换掉 cluster-based 的 14 类。用 sc.tl.score_genes() 给每个细胞打 6 个 Neftel 模块分数，然后取 max → 干净的 6-7 类。

Copilot 2026/04/19 09:01

现在在 cell 23（cluster-based tumor_annot）后面插入一个新的 scoring-based 注释 cell，替代那个混乱的 14 类方案：

▸ Tool calls (1)
edit_notebook_file 
{
  "filePath": "/Users/yuzuan/Downloads/生信技能树月更复现/scGBM/4_Sub_clustering.ipynb",
  "editType": "insert",
  "cellId": "#VSC-6dfacf26",
  "language": "python",
  "newCode": "# Per-cell scoring: 用 Neftel 6 模块分数取 max，替代 cluster-based 注释\nneftel_modules = {\n    \"MES1\":  [\"VIM\", \"LDHA\", \"ENO2\", \"ANXA1\", \"COL1A2\", \"TNC\", \"ZFP36L1\"],\n    \"MES2\":  [\"HILPDA\", \"DDIT3\", \"HSPB1\", \"GPR37L1\", \"COL11A1\", \"PDLIM4\"],\n    \"AC\":    [\"S100B\", \"GFAP\", \"SLC1A3\", \"MLC1\", \"HOPX\", \"ATP1A2\", \"CHL1\", \"CPNE1\"],\n    \"OPC\":   [\"OLIG1\", \"OMG\", \"PLP1\", \"PLLP\", \"TNR\", \"ALCAM\", \"SOX10\", \"BEX4\"],\n    \"NPC1\":  [\"SOX4\", \"SOX11\", \"DCX\", \"BEX1\", \"LSM3\", \"PLAT\"],\n    \"NPC2\":  [\"STMN1\", \"STMN2\", \"STMN4\", \"DLX6-AS1\", \"GAD1\"],\n}\n\n# 打分\navailable = set(adata_tum.var_names)\nfor mod, genes in neftel_modules.items():\n    genes_use = [g for g in genes if g in available]\n    sc.tl.score_genes(adata_tum, gene_list=genes_use, score_name=f'Neftel_{mod}', use_raw=False)\n    print(f\"{mod}: {len(genes_use)}/{len(genes)} genes\")\n\n# 取每个细胞的最高分模块\nscore_cols = [f'Neftel_{m}' for m in neftel_modules]\nscore_df = adata_tum.obs[score_cols].copy()\nadata_tum.obs['Neftel_state'] = score_df.idxmax(axis=1).str.replace('Neftel_', '')\n\n# 标记 Cycling (MKI67/TOP2A 高表达)\ncycling_genes = ['MKI67', 'TOP2A', 'CENPF']\ncycling_use = [g for g in cycling_genes if g in available]\nsc.tl.score_genes(adata_tum, gene_list=cycling_use, score_name='Cycling_score', use_raw=False)\ncycling_mask = adata_tum.obs['Cycling_score'] > 1.0  # 严格阈值\nadata_tum.obs.loc[cycling_mask, 'Neftel_state'] = adata_tum.obs.loc[cycling_mask, 'Neftel_state'] + '-Cycling'\n\n# 覆盖 tumor_subtype\nadata_tum.obs['tumor_subtype'] = adata_tum.obs['Neftel_state'].astype('category')\nprint(\"\\n--- Per-cell Neftel assignment ---\")\nprint(adata_tum.obs['tumor_subtype'].value_counts())"
}

Copilot 2026/04/19 09:26

明白，确实还是混杂。问题在于 per-cell scoring 导致"盐胡椒"效应——相邻细胞各自取 max 分数，边界不清晰。

改用 **cluster-level majority voting**：先 per-cell 打分，再在每个 leiden cluster 内取均分最高的状态 → 同一 cluster 统一标签，边界干净。

▸ Tool calls (1)
read_file 
{
  "endLine": 298,
  "filePath": "/Users/yuzuan/Downloads/生信技能树月更复现/scGBM/4_Sub_clustering.ipynb",
  "startLine": 261
}
Copilot 2026/04/19 09:27

5 个干净类别，没有 MES2（被其他状态覆盖）和 Cycling（阈值未触发）。画 UMAP 看效果：

▸ Tool calls (1)
run_notebook_cell 
{
  "cellId": "#VSC-dbafa803",
  "filePath": "/Users/yuzuan/Downloads/生信技能树月更复现/scGBM/4_Sub_clustering.ipynb"
}
Copilot 2026/04/19 09:28

效果显著改善。Cluster-level majority voting 消除了"盐胡椒"混杂效应——每个 leiden cluster 统一着色，边界清晰。5 个状态空间分布清楚：

- **AC** (蓝)：中部+右侧多个簇
- **MES1** (红)：上方+下方，明确的间充质区域
- **OPC** (绿)：左侧+左下
- **NPC1** (紫)：右下角独立
- **NPC2** (棕)：左下角独立

MES2 未被任何 cluster 判定为最高分（被 MES1 覆盖），Cycling cluster 也低于阈值。这在 Neftel 框架下合理——MES2 通常是 MES1 的子态。

vscode_askQuestions 
{
  "questions": [
    {
      "header": "UMAP满意度",
      "question": "Cluster-level majority voting 后 UMAP 是否满意？接下来想怎么做？",

Copilot 2026/04/19 09:34

**Harmony 整合后效果极好！** UMAP 现在呈现经典的 GBM 状态连续体结构：

- **AC** (蓝) — 上方 + 右侧大片连续区域
- **OPC** (绿) — 左侧连续区域
- **MES1** (红) — 中部紧凑区域
- **NPC1** (紫) — 下方独立簇
- **NPC2** (棕) — 左下方，与 OPC 相邻

状态之间平滑过渡（AC↔OPC, AC↔MES1, OPC↔NPC2），完全符合 Neftel et al. 2019 的四态连续模型。之前的碎片化完全是 sample batch effect 导致的。
